      "description": "<h2>Titan Magazines</h2><p>Titan Magazines mostly print comic reprints of US titles and/or licensed properties for UK and Irish store shelves. These include their long association with DC Comics and popular sci-fi and fantasy franchises such as Star Trek, <a href=\"https://www.comicvine.com/star-wars-galaxy/4050-36522/\" data-ref-id=\"4050-36522\">Star Wars</a>, <a href=\"https://www.comicvine.com/transformers-robots-in-disguise/4050-32852/\" data-ref-id=\"4050-32852\">The Transformers</a>, Supernatural, <a href=\"https://www.comicvine.com/the-walking-dead-the-official-magazine/4050-53365/\" data-ref-id=\"4050-53365\">The Walking Dead</a> and Buffy. They also publish the UK comics magazine <i><a href=\"/clint/4050-35191/\" data-ref-id=\"4050-35191\">CLiNT</a> </i>and<i><a href=\"/tank-girl-carioca/4050-56273/\" data-ref-id=\"4050-56273\"> Tank Girl</a>. </i>They also publish a kids line of magazines including Dora, Barbie, Monster High, and <a href=\"/star-wars-the-clone-wars/4050-40416/\" data-ref-id=\"4050-40416\">Clone Wars.</a></p><h2>Titan Books</h2><p>Titan Books are the primary publisher of US comic books in the United Kingdom, mostly printing licensed franchises, including <a href=\"/dc-comics/4010-10/\" data-ref-id=\"4010-10\">DC Comics</a> characters which they often print special Titan editions of TPBs and OGNs, and also, the <a href=\"/the-simpsons-annual/4050-55679/\" data-ref-id=\"4050-55679\">ann</a><a href=\"/bart-simpson-annual/4050-55682/\" data-ref-id=\"4050-55682\">uals</a> and TPBs of <a href=\"/the-simpsons/4060-46071/\" data-ref-id=\"4060-46071\">The Simpsons</a> and <a href=\"/marvel-uk/4010-2812/\" data-ref-id=\"4010-2812\">Marvel UK</a>'s <a href=\"/the-transformers/4050-20559/\" data-ref-id=\"4050-20559\">The Transformers</a>.</p><h2>Titan Comics</h2><p>Originally comics were printed under the Titan Magazines and trades under <a href=\"/titan-books/4010-387/\" data-ref-id=\"4010-387\">Titan Books</a>. In 2013 Titan created the comics imprint to publish original creator-owned comics alongside new and classic graphic novels!</p><p>The imprint will launch in July 2013 with two creator-owned miniseries and four new collections, with a new series beginning each month afterwards:</p><ul><li><a href=\"//www.comicvine.com/chronos-commandos-1-dawn-patrol/4000-417024/\" data-ref-id=\"4000-417024\"><b>Chronos Commandos: Dawn Patrol</b></a> by writer/artist <a href=\"/stuart-jennett/4040-55861/\" data-ref-id=\"4040-55861\">Stuart Jennett</a> (Marvel UK)</li><li><a href=\"//www.comicvine.com/number-cruncher-1/4000-417033/\" data-ref-id=\"4000-417033\"><b>Numbercruncher</b></a> by <a href=\"/x-men-legacy/4050-20691/\" data-ref-id=\"4050-20691\"><i>X-Men: Legacy</i></a> writer Si Spurrier and <a href=\"/2000ad/4010-2358/\" data-ref-id=\"4010-2358\"><i>2000AD</i></a> artist <a href=\"/paul-j-holden/4040-48853/\" data-ref-id=\"4040-48853\">P.J. Holden</a></li><li><b>Ring of Roses</b> – collected in color for the first time, by writer Das Petrou and artist <a href=\"/john-watkiss/4040-2628/\" data-ref-id=\"4040-2628\">John Watkiss</a></li><li><a href=\"//www.comicvine.com/thrud-the-barbarian/4050-67720/\" data-ref-id=\"4050-67720\"><b>Thrud The Barbarian</b></a> by writer/artist <a href=\"/carl-critchlow/4040-24939/\" data-ref-id=\"4040-24939\">Carl Critchlow</a> (<i><a href=\"/2000ad/4010-2358/\" data-ref-id=\"4010-2358\">2000AD</a>, <a href=\"/magic-the-gathering/4050-45576/\" data-ref-id=\"4050-45576\">Magic: The Gathering</a></i>)</li><li><b>The First Kingdom</b> by comic legend <a href=\"/jack-katz/4040-37728/\" data-ref-id=\"4040-37728\">Jack Katz</a></li></ul><p>The second wave will see three new series launching later in the year:</p><p>September</p><ul><li><b>Gravestown</b> by writer <a href=\"/roger-gibson/4040-65719/\" data-ref-id=\"4040-65719\">Roger Gibson</a> and artist Vince Danks (<a href=\"/harker/4050-52164/\" data-ref-id=\"4050-52164\"><i>Harker</i></a>)</li><li><b>Surface Tension</b> by writer/artist Jay Gunn</li></ul><p>October</p><ul><li><a href=\"//www.comicvine.com/death-sentence/4050-62407/\" data-ref-id=\"4050-62407\"><b>Death Sentence</b></a> by writer Monty Nero and artist Mike Dowling (<i><a href=\"/2000ad/4010-2358/\" data-ref-id=\"4010-2358\">2000AD</a>, Rex Royd</i>)</li></ul>",
